(*******************************************************************************

 The projection

 Given a strict functor `F : C ⟶ StrictCat`, then we have a projection going
 from `∫ F` to `C`.
 In addition, the Grothendieck construction is pseudofunctorial.

 Contents
 1. The projection
 2. Action on 1-cells
 3. Action on 2-cells
 4. Identitor
 5. Compositor

 *******************************************************************************)

 1. The projection

C: setcategory

C: setcategory
F: C ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
∏ a b : total_setcategory_of_set_functor F,
total_setcategory_of_set_functor F ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ C ⟦ ?F a, ?F b ⟧

  
C: setcategory
F: C ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
total_setcategory_of_set_functor F → C
 exact (λ x, pr1 x).
  
C: setcategory
F: C ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
∏ a b : total_setcategory_of_set_functor F,
total_setcategory_of_set_functor F ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ C
  ⟦ (λ x : total_setcategory_of_set_functor F, pr1 x)
      a,
  (λ x : total_setcategory_of_set_functor F, pr1 x) b
  ⟧
 exact (λ _ _ f, pr1 f).
Defined.

(**
 2. Action on 1-cells

Section FunctorTotalCategoryFromSetFunctor.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : setcategory}
          (F : C₁ ⟶ C₂)
          {G₁ : C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory}
          {G₂ : C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory}
          (α : G₁ ⟹ F ∙ G₂).

  
C₁, C₂: setcategory
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F ∙ G₂
x, y: total_precategory_of_set_functor G₁
f: total_precategory_of_set_functor G₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
pr1 (# G₂ (# F (pr1 f))) (pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)) =
pr1 (α (pr1 y)) (pr1 (# G₁ (pr1 f)) (pr2 x))

  
C₁, C₂: setcategory
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F ∙ G₂
x, y: total_precategory_of_set_functor G₁
f: total_precategory_of_set_functor G₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
pr1 (# G₂ (# F (pr1 f))) (pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)) =
pr1 (α (pr1 y)) (pr1 (# G₁ (pr1 f)) (pr2 x))

    exact (!(eqtohomot (maponpaths (λ z, pr11 z) (nat_trans_ax α _ _ (pr1 f))) (pr2 x))).
  Qed.

     F (pr1 x),, pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)) a,

   F (pr1 x),, pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)) b ⟧
 
C₁, C₂: setcategory
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F ∙ G₂
x, y: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁
f: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
G₂ (pr1 (F (pr1 y),, pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 y)) (pr2 y)))
⟦ pr1 (# G₂ (# F (pr1 f)))
    (pr2 (F (pr1 x),, pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 x)) (pr2 x))),
pr2 (F (pr1 y),, pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 y)) (pr2 y)) ⟧

      exact (idtoiso (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq f)
             · # (pr1 (α (pr1 y))) (pr2 f)).
  Defined.

     ?Goal0)
· pr1
    (idtoiso
       (eq_in_set_fiber (functor_id G₂ (F (pr1 x)))
          (pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 x)) (pr2 x))))

       (maponpaths (α (pr1 z))
          (eq_in_set_fiber
             (functor_comp G₁ (pr1 f) (pr1 g)) (pr2 x))))

                   (maponpaths

· idtoiso (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq g)

 exact (λ x, identity _).

   identity
     ((pr1_total_category_of_set_functor G₁ ∙ F) x))

         exact (id_right _ @ !(id_left _))).
  Defined.

    apply identity_is_z_iso.
  Defined.
End FunctorTotalCategoryFromSetFunctor.

F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
α: F₁ ⟹ F₂
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
β₁: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β₂: G₁ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₂
p: ∏ x : C₁,
pr1 β₁ x ∙ # (pr1 G₂) (pr1 α x) = pr1 β₂ x
x, y: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁
f: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
pr1
  (idtoiso
     (eq_in_set_fiber
        (functor_comp G₂ (# F₁ (pr1 f)) (α (pr1 y)))
        (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x))))
· (# (# G₂ (α (pr1 y)))
     (idtoiso
        (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq F₁
           β₁ f))
   · # (# G₂ (α (pr1 y)))
       (# (pr1 (β₁ (pr1 y))) (pr2 f))
   · idtoiso
       (nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_eq y)) =
idtoiso
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 C₂ ⟦ F₁ (pr1 x), F₂ (pr1 y) ⟧,
      pr1 (# G₂ z) (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)))
     (nat_trans_ax α (pr1 x) (pr1 y) (pr1 f)))
· (pr1
     (idtoiso
        (eq_in_set_fiber
           (functor_comp G₂ (α (pr1 x)) (# F₂ (pr1 f)))
           (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x))))
   · (# (pr1 (# G₂ (# F₂ (pr1 f))))
        (idtoiso
           (nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_eq
              x))
      · (idtoiso
           (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq
              F₂ β₂ f) · # (pr1 (β₂ (pr1 y))) (pr2 f))))

     (λ z : pr1 C₂ ⟦ F₁ (pr1 x), F₂ (pr1 y) ⟧,
      pr1 (# G₂ z) (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)))
     (nat_trans_ax α (pr1 x) (pr1 y) (pr1 f)))
· pr1
    (idtoiso
       (eq_in_set_fiber
          (functor_comp G₂ (α (pr1 x)) (# F₂ (pr1 f)))
          (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x))))
· # (pr1 (# G₂ (# F₂ (pr1 f))))
    (idtoiso
       (nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_eq x))
· idtoiso
    (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq F₂ β₂ f) =
?y'

     (((maponpaths

           pr1 (# G₂ z) (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)))
          (nat_trans_ax α (pr1 x) (pr1 y) (pr1 f)) @
        eq_in_set_fiber
          (functor_comp G₂ (α (pr1 x)) (# F₂ (pr1 f)))
          (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x))) @
       maponpaths (# G₂ (# F₂ (pr1 f)))
         (nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_eq x)) @
      functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq F₂ β₂ f))
· # (pr1 (β₂ (pr1 y))) (pr2 f) =
pr1
  (idtoiso
     (eq_in_set_fiber
        (functor_comp G₂ (# F₁ (pr1 f)) (α (pr1 y)))
        (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)) @
      maponpaths (# G₂ (α (pr1 y)))
        (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq F₁
           β₁ f)))
· # (# G₂ (α (pr1 y))) (# (pr1 (β₁ (pr1 y))) (pr2 f))
· idtoiso
    (nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_eq y)

       (pr1 (# G₁ (pr1 f)) (pr2 x)))
· # (pr1 β₂ (pr1 y)) (pr2 f)
· pr1
    (idtoiso
       (! path_functor_ob (p (pr1 y)) (pr2 y) @
        nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_eq y)) =
?b
C₁, C₂: setcategory
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
α: F₁ ⟹ F₂
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
β₁: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β₂: G₁ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₂
p: ∏ x : C₁,
pr1 β₁ x ∙ # (pr1 G₂) (pr1 α x) = pr1 β₂ x
x, y: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁
f: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
?b =
pr1
  (idtoiso
     (((maponpaths
          (λ z : pr1 C₂ ⟦ F₁ (pr1 x), F₂ (pr1 y) ⟧,
           pr1 (# G₂ z) (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)))
          (nat_trans_ax α (pr1 x) (pr1 y) (pr1 f)) @
        eq_in_set_fiber
          (functor_comp G₂ (α (pr1 x)) (# F₂ (pr1 f)))
          (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x))) @
       maponpaths (# G₂ (# F₂ (pr1 f)))
         (nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_eq x)) @
      functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq F₂ β₂ f))
· # (pr1 (β₂ (pr1 y))) (pr2 f)

      
C₁, C₂: setcategory
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
α: F₁ ⟹ F₂

     (eq_in_set_fiber
        (functor_comp G₂ (# F₁ (pr1 f)) (α (pr1 y)))
        (pr1 (pr1 β₁ (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)) @

· idtoiso

       (! path_functor_ob (p (pr1 y)) (pr2 y) @
        nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_eq y)) =
?b

⟹ functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β₂

  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ β₁)
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β₂)

G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
β₁: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β₂: G₁ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₂
p: ∏ x : C₁,
pr1 β₁ x ∙ # (pr1 G₂) (pr1 α x) = pr1 β₂ x
is_nat_trans
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ β₁)
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β₂) ?t

    
C₁, C₂: setcategory
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
α: F₁ ⟹ F₂
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
β₁: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β₂: G₁ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₂
p: ∏ x : C₁,
pr1 β₁ x ∙ # (pr1 G₂) (pr1 α x) = pr1 β₂ x
nat_trans_data
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ β₁)
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β₂)
 exact nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_data.
    
C₁, C₂: setcategory
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
α: F₁ ⟹ F₂
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
β₁: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β₂: G₁ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₂
p: ∏ x : C₁,
pr1 β₁ x ∙ # (pr1 G₂) (pr1 α x) = pr1 β₂ x
is_nat_trans
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ β₁)
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β₂)
  nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_data
 exact nat_trans_total_category_of_set_functor_is_nat_trans.
  Defined.
End NatTransTotalCategoryFromNatTrans.

(**
 5. Compositor
 *)
Definition functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp_data
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : setcategory}
           {F₁ : C₁ ⟶ C₂}
           {F₂ : C₂ ⟶ C₃}
           {G₁ : C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory}
           {G₂ : C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory}
           {G₃ : C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory}
           (α : G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂)
           (β : G₂ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₃)
  : nat_trans_data
      (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ α
       ∙ functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β)
      (functor_total_category_of_set_functor
         (F₁ ∙ F₂)
         (nat_trans_comp _ _ _ α (pre_whisker F₁ β)))
  := λ _, identity _.


C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₃: C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β: G₂ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₃
is_nat_trans
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ α
   ∙ functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β)
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor (F₁ ∙ F₂)
     (nat_trans_comp G₁ (F₁ ∙ G₂)
        (functor_composite_data F₁ (F₂ ∙ G₃)) α
        (pre_whisker F₁ β)))
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp_data
     α β)


C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₃: C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β: G₂ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₃
is_nat_trans
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ α
   ∙ functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β)
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor (F₁ ∙ F₂)
     (nat_trans_comp G₁ (F₁ ∙ G₂)
        (functor_composite_data F₁ (F₂ ∙ G₃)) α
        (pre_whisker F₁ β)))
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp_data
     α β)

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₃: C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β: G₂ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₃
x, y: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁
f: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
# (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ α
   ∙ functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β) f
· functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp_data α
    β y =
functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp_data α β
  x
· # (functor_total_category_of_set_functor (F₁ ∙ F₂)
       (nat_trans_comp G₁ (F₁ ∙ G₂)
          (functor_composite_data F₁ (F₂ ∙ G₃)) α
          (pre_whisker F₁ β))) f

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₃: C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β: G₂ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₃
x, y: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁
f: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
# (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ α
   ∙ functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β) f =
# (functor_total_category_of_set_functor (F₁ ∙ F₂)
     (nat_trans_comp G₁ (F₁ ∙ G₂)
        (functor_composite_data F₁ (F₂ ∙ G₃)) α
        (pre_whisker F₁ β))) f

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₃: C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory

f: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
# F₂ (# F₁ (pr1 f)) = # F₂ (# F₁ (pr1 f))
C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₃: C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory

f: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
idtoiso
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq F₂ β
     (# F₁ (pr1 f),,
      idtoiso
        (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq F₁ α
           f) · # (pr1 (α (pr1 y))) (pr2 f)))
· # (pr1 (β (F₁ (pr1 y))))
    (idtoiso
       (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq F₁ α
          f) · # (pr1 (α (pr1 y))) (pr2 f)) =
idtoiso
  (maponpaths
     (λ z : pr1 C₃ ⟦ F₂ (F₁ (pr1 x)), F₂ (F₁ (pr1 y))
            ⟧,
      pr1 (# G₃ z)
        (pr1 (pr1 β (F₁ (pr1 x)))
           (pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 x)) (pr2 x)))) ?Goal)
· (idtoiso
     (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq
        (F₁ ∙ F₂)
        (nat_trans_comp G₁
           (functor_composite_data F₁ G₂)
           (functor_composite_data F₁
              (functor_composite_data F₂ G₃)) α
           (pre_whisker F₁ β)) f)
   · # (pr1 β (pr1 F₁ (pr1 y)))
       (# (α (pr1 y)) (pr2 f)))

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory

 apply idpath.

  (maponpaths

           (pr1 (pr1 α (pr1 x)) (pr2 x))))
     (idpath (# F₂ (# F₁ (pr1 f)))))
· (idtoiso

           (functor_composite_data F₁
              (functor_composite_data F₂ G₃)) α
           (pre_whisker F₁ β)) f)
   · # (pr1 β (pr1 F₁ (pr1 y)))
       (# (α (pr1 y)) (pr2 f)))
 
C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory

       (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq F₁ α

       (# (α (pr1 y)) (pr2 f)))

          f) · # (pr1 (α (pr1 y))) (pr2 f)) =

  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_eq (F₁ ∙ F₂)
     (nat_trans_comp G₁ (functor_composite_data F₁ G₂)
        (functor_composite_data F₁
           (functor_composite_data F₂ G₃)) α
        (pre_whisker F₁ β)) f)
· # (pr1 β (pr1 F₁ (pr1 y))) (# (α (pr1 y)) (pr2 f))

        (pre_whisker F₁ β)) f)

    apply setcategory_eq_idtoiso.
Qed.

β: G₂ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₃
is_nat_trans
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₁ α
   ∙ functor_total_category_of_set_functor F₂ β)
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor (F₁ ∙ F₂)
     (nat_trans_comp G₁ (F₁ ∙ G₂)
        (functor_composite_data F₁ (F₂ ∙ G₃)) α
        (pre_whisker F₁ β)))
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp_data
     α β)
 exact (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp_is_nat_trans α β).
Defined.


C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₃: C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β: G₂ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₃
is_nat_z_iso
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp α β)


C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₃: C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β: G₂ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₃
is_nat_z_iso
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp α β)

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: setcategory
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
G₁: C₁ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₂: C₂ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
G₃: C₃ ⟶ cat_of_setcategory
α: G₁ ⟹ F₁ ∙ G₂
β: G₂ ⟹ F₂ ∙ G₃
c: total_setcategory_of_set_functor G₁
is_z_isomorphism
  (functor_total_category_of_set_functor_on_comp α β c)

  apply identity_is_z_iso.
Defined.
